34:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":["For Swagger 2 documents, ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"OpenApiConverter.upgradeDocument"}]," composes each server URL from ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"schemes"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"host"}],", and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"basePath"}]," and rejects endpoint fields containing queries or fragments. Equivalent host casing and root URL spellings with and without a trailing slash normalize to one Swagger endpoint. An operation’s ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"schemes"}],", ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"consumes"}],", and ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"produces"}]," override the document defaults; when neither media list is present, the converter uses ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"application/json"}]," for compatibility. An explicit empty media list clears the inherited default, but it cannot accompany a body or response payload because the emended content model has no media key under which to retain that schema or example. Swagger ",["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"formData"}]," parameters become one object-shaped request body; scalar enums, nullable scalar or array fields, and recursively nested arrays of those scalar shapes remain simple form fields. 35:["$","p",null,{"className":"x:not-first:mt-[1.25em] x:leading-7","children":[["$","code",null,{"className":"nextra-code","dir":"ltr","children":"OpenApiConverter.downgradeDocument(document, \"2.0\")"}]," keeps media types on each operation instead of guessing shared document defaults.
